l1,solora,a,size,getinfo,ted,key,filebrute,workspace=table.insert,y,string.len,string.sub,type,table.concat,{z=5,b=4,B=44,m=47,i=1,W=35,[`1`]=57,L=7,E=53,C=59,D=31,d=48,Z=18,p=60,H=32,y=37,[`3`]=9,X=16,[`/`]=55,j=46,e=61,[`8`]=6,G=39,c=15,u=33,[`+`]=54,N=22,I=58,T=12,J=0,l=36,x=23,a=49,q=11,[`2`]=34,v=8,U=43,[`7`]=25,[`5`]=62,P=2,[`0`]=41,f=30,[`9`]=14,g=26,A=40,[`6`]=38,k=52,h=13,R=63,w=21,n=45,r=28,F=56,M=3,o=19,t=27,Y=10,V=51,[`4`]=29,Q=20,s=24,S=17,O=50,K=42},math.floor,string.char for y=1,#solora,1 do local I=(solora)[y]if getinfo(I)==`string`then local getinfo,PandaAuth,rScriptsIsBad,BaconBoss,red=a(I),{},1,0,0 while rScriptsIsBad<=getinfo do local solora=size(I,rScriptsIsBad,rScriptsIsBad)local a=(key)[solora]if a then BaconBoss=BaconBoss+a*64^(3-red)red=red+1 if red==4 then red=0 local
